 rajya sarkaar ke vakil anil sakhaare ne adaalat main kaha ki sibiai ke paas maamle kii jaanch kaa adhikaar nahin he kyonki na to rajya sarkaar ne or naa hi ucch nyaayalay ne use maamle kii jaanch saunpi
 a division bench of Justice SA Bobde and Justice Mridula Bhatkar directed Sakhare to file an affidavit stating that the state government had not given its consent to the CBI to probe the scam
 sakhaare ne kaha, ‘‘ek nyaayik ayog ne pehle hi report jamaa kar di he jisamen kaha gaya he ki jis jameen par adarsh houseing sosayadi kii imaarat bani he vah rajya sarkaar kii he or raksha mantralay kii nahin he
 So CBI does not figure in the picture
 dilli police vishesh pratishthan adhinium ke tahat sibiai banaai gayi thi or uske anusaar agency tabhi maamle kii jaanch kar sakati he jab rajya sarkaar yaa ucch nyaayalay use tafteesh kaa kaam de
 '' adarsh sosayadi kii ore se varisht vakil shekhar nafade ne bhi daleel di ki sibiai ke paas maamle kii jaanch kaa adhikaar nahin he
 The court also directed the society to file an application on this
 sibiai ne 30 april ko pichhali sunwaayee ke dauraan adaalat ko aashwaasan diya tha ki vah maamle main 15 june tak aaropapatr daakhil karegi
 The agency said today that it will submit the charge sheet in 10 days
 sibiai ke vakil ejaj khan ne adaalat ko bataaya, ‘‘jaanch antim str par he
 The chargesheet will be filed in 10 days
 ’’ iske baad adaalat ne sunwaayee chaar july tak taal di
 The CBI launched an investigation into the Adarsh scam in 2010 on the instructions of the Ministry of Defense
 janvari, 2011 main agency ne maamle main purv mukhyamantri ashok chavaan samet 14 logon ke khilaaf maamla darj kiya tha, jinamein sevanivrutt sainya adhikari, netaa or naukarshah hai
 The comments maamle ke nau aropiyon ko isi saal march main giraftaar kiya gaya tha lekin baad main jamaanat par chhod diya gaya
 The CBI could not file a charge sheet against him within the stipulated period of 60 days
 jin nau aropiyon ko jamaanat di gayi thi, unamem iees adhikari pradeep vyas, shahari vikaas vibhaag main purv up sachiv pivi deshmukh, brigadier (sevanivrutt) mem vaanchu, sevanivrutt raksha sampada adhikari aarasi thakur, major general (sevanivrutt) eaar kumaar, major general (sevanivrutt) tike kaul or purv vidhaan parishad sadsy kanhaiyalaal gidwani hai
 Apart from criminal conspiracy on the accused, the Prevention of Corruption Act and Benami Transaction (prohibition) were charged under various sections of the law
 maamle main sibiai ke alaava pravartan nideshaalay or iskar vibhaag bhi aniyamittaaon kii jaanch kar rahe hai

 nyaayamurti ese bobade or nyaayamurti mridula bhatkar kii khandpeeth ne sakhaare ko ek halafanama daakhil karne kaa nirdesh diya jisamen yah ullekh ho ki rajya sarkaar ne sibiai ko ghotaale kii jaanch ke liye apni sahmati nahin di
 Sakhare said, "A judicial commission has already submitted the report which states that the land on which the Adarsh housing Society building is built belongs to the state government and not to the defense ministry
" isliye sibiai tasviir main nahin aati
 The CBI was created under the Delhi Police Special Establishment Act and according to that the agency can investigate the case only when the state government or the High Court assigns it to the investigation
 ’’ On behalf of Adarsh society, senior advocate Shekhar Nafade also argued that the CBI does not have the authority to investigate the case
 adaalat ne sosayadi ko bhi is par aavedan daakhil karne kaa nirdesh diya
 The CBI, during its previous hearing on April 30, assured the court that it would file a chargesheet in the case by June 15
 agency ne aaj kaha ki vah aaropapatr 10 din main jamaa karegi
 CBI counsel Ejaz Khan told the court, "the investigation is at a final stage
 aaropapatr 10 din main daakhil kar diya jayega
 The court then adjourned the hearing till July 4
 sibiai ne raksha mantralay ke nirdeshon par 2010 main adarsh ghotaale kii jaanch shuru kii thi
 In January 2011, the agency registered a case in the case against 14 people, including former Chief Minister Ashok Chavan, including retired military officers, leaders and bureaucrats
 tippaniyan Nine accused in the case were arrested in March this year but later released on bail
 sibiai unke khilaaf 60 din kii niyat avadhi main aaropapatr daakhil nahin kar pai thi
 The nine accused, who were granted bail, include IAS officer Pradeep Vyas, former Deputy Secretary in Urban Development Department PV Deshmukh, Brigadier (retd) MM Wanchoo, retired defense estate officer RC Thakur, Major General (retd) AR Kumar, Major General ( Retired) TK Kaul and former Legislative Council member Kanhaiyalal Gidwani

 Besides the CBI, the Enforcement Directorate and the Income Tax Department are also investigating the irregularities

 gujarat kii ek adaalat dwaara 2002 danga maamle main narendra modi ko clin chit die jane kii bhaajapa ne naitik jeet bataate hue prashansa kii he, jabaki congress ne kaha ki kanoonee raste kaa vikalp ab bhi khulaa he, vahiin vamadalon ne ise durbhagyapurna bataaya he
 Welcoming the court order, the BJP targeted the Congress and said that the party wants to implicate Modi in a criminal case as it cannot fight politically
 rajyasabha main vipaksh ke netaa pratipaksh arun jetali ne kaha ki farji bayaanbaji saboot nahin ban sakate hai
 a fundamental difference between untruth and truth is that all facts remain together with truth, while untruth falls apart
 unhone kaha ki gujarat ke 2002 ke dangon ke silsile main narendra modi ko clin chit die jane se bhaajapa ke is vichaar kii pushti hui he ki ye aarope prachaar or raajnneetik drushti se lagaae gaye or isamen koi tathy nahin the
 He said, we have no hesitation in saying that the Congress party cannot fight any political battle against Narendra Modi, so has been doing such propaganda
 jetali ne kaha, pichley 11 varshon main congress party or uske mitra enjio ke dushprachaar se modi aprabhavit rahe or is dauraan 2002, 2007 or 2012 ke rajya chunaav main jabardast jeet darj kii
 He said that after proving political and administrative efficiency, the judiciary today has also confirmed that Modi has been declared clean
 yah bhaajapa or narendra modi kii naitik jeet he
 It is noteworthy that giving a big relief to Modi, the metropolitan court rejected the petition of Zakia Jafri filed against the Special Investigation Team giving him a clean chit in the 2002 riots case
 jetali ne kaha ki is faisle se kuch logon ke ve aarope galat sabit hue hai, jisamen kaha gaya tha ki gujarat dangon main modi kii bhoomika thi
 On the court's decision, Union Minister Kapil Sibal has said that he can understand the pain of the victims
 sibbal ke bayaan par jetali ne kaha, ham sab log sabhi dangon ke peediton ke dard ko samajhate hai, jisamen 1984 ke dangon ke peedit bhi shaamil hai
 He said that this is the first incident after independence when a Chief Minister set up a commission of inquiry against him after being accused
 iske baad gujarat police ne jaanch kii, phir vishesh jaanch dal (esaiti) ne jaanch kii or iske supreme court, nyaay mitra ne jaanch kii
 Jaitley said, Modi has come out innocent after so much investigation
 congress ke log isaki tulana 1984 ke sikh virdohi dange se karke dekh sakate hai
 On the other hand, the Congress said that it should not be held that the court verdict is a 'confirmation' of the clean chit given to Chief Minister Narendra Modi in connection with the 2002 Gujarat riots and that all legal options are still open to the complainant in this case
 congress pravaktaa abhishek singhvi ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki shikayatakarta is aadesh ko chunauti dene kii hakdaar hai
 For the BJP, to consider this decision as the last word on judicial facts or to confirm it is wrong and completely misleading

 vijay ne maukey kii najaakat ke anuroop ballebaaji kii or apana chauthaa tathaa videshi sarajameen par pehla shatak lagaaya

 unki pari main 20 chauke or ek chakka shaamil he

 dhoni kii 64 gend kii pari main paanch chauke shaamil hai

 For England, James Anderson took two for 70, while Stuart Broad took 26 and Liam Plunkett took one wicket for 56 runs
 vijay kaa saath dene ke liye pujaara krij par utre or donon ne sahajata ke saath pari aage badhaayi

 Aziz Qureshi won the election
 is seat par 1980 main rajya ke purv siem sunderlaal patwa bhi jeet chuke hai

 vahiin 5 baar is seat parabijepico jeet mili

 sarkaar ne iviem mashin par sawaal uthaane vaale netaaon kii bolti band karne vaala kadam uthaa liya he
 The next Lok Sabha election of the country to be held in the year 2019 will be entirely through Voter Vefiable Paper Audit Trail machines
 vivipat mashin se voter khud hi yah dekh sakegaa ki usne jisko vot diya tha usee ko vot mila yaa nahin
 When needed, it can also be counted again with the result of EVM by counting again with the slip generated while casting the vote
 aapako bataa den ki centre sarkaar ne buudhvaar ko vivipat mashiinon kii kharid ke liye 3,174 karod rupye ke fund ko manjuuri de di he
 In the cabinet meeting, the government decided that this amount will be provided to the Central Election Commission for the purchase of 16 lakh 15 thousand VVPAT machines
 gauratlab he ki centre sarkaar ne ye faisla aise samay par liya he jab vidhansabha chunaav ke nateezon ke baad bispi, aam aadmi party, samaajawaadee party or congress samet kai vipakshi dalon neiviem mashinako lekar sawaal uthaae the or kaha tha ki ho saktaa he bijepi ko jitaane ke liye in mashiinon main chhedchhad kii gai ho
 However, both the government and the Election Commission had repeatedly said that EVM machines are completely reliable and impossible to tamper with
 darasal prayog ke taur par vivipat mashiinon kaa istemaal 2013 se shuru ho gaya he, lekin bade paimaane par ise chunaav main istemaal kiye jane ke liye lakhon mashiinon kii jarurat he jiske liye niwarchan ayog lambey samay se dhan kii maang kar rahaa tha
 In a letter written to the Law Ministry on 22 March, the Election Commission had said that it would not be appropriate to buy VVPAT machines in view of the manner in which the question of EVM machines is being raised in the current environment
 niwarchan ayog kaa kahana tha ki agar 2019 main vivipat mashine se chunaav karana he to abhi se mashiinon kii kharid ke liye order dena hoga
 Giving information about the cabinet decision, Finance Minister Arun Jaitley said that now these machines will be delivered to the Election Commission by September 2018
 jetali se jab poocha gaya ki kya vipakshi partiyon ke dabaav main ye faisla kiya gaya he to unhone kaha ki mashiinon par sawaal uthaane se haarane vaali partiyon kaa nateeja badal nahin jayega

 twitter
 com / dwa6xhfslv bihar ke ek dak tikat sangrahakarta ne pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa chaar tikaton kaa ek set banwaaya he
 This set of postage stamps is the vision of Pradeep Jain, a famous collector of Bihar
 pradeep jain ne bataaya, in dak tikat or vishesh aavaran kii pariklpana narendra modi ke pradhanmantri banane kii ore agrasar hote vakt kii gayi
 It was a very popular event and not only his country but the whole world was watching him with keenness
 jain ne bataaya ki in dak tikaton ko gat 26 may ko dak vibhaag kii maai stamp shrinkhalaa ke tahat banwaaya gaya he
 The four postage stamps, priced at five rupees, depict Modi in a smile and attach him to the bunches of various Indian flowers Kumudini, Pansi, Dahlia and Cinerea
 vishesh aavaran par jain samudaay ke navkar mantra chapa hua he or us par modi ko muskaraate hue puure khile hue camel se nikalate hue chitrit kiya gaya he, jiskaa sheershak namo kii shakti he
 These postage stamps and special covers were taken to Delhi by a senior BJP leader and presented it to Modi and BJP President Rajnath Singh
 sambhavat: isse prabhavit hokar videsh mantralay ne pradeep jain se in dak tikaton ko kuch padosi deshon main bhejne ke liye sampark saadhaa he
 Jain said that he got the idea in 2009 of US President Barack Obama issuing postage stamp in Washington that if the American people can do it then why can't we
 pradeep jain landan ke royal philatelic socity ke sadsy hai or austria ke insbark main sthit international associyeshan of philatelic export main ekmaatr bhartiya hai
 He downloaded Modi's picture from the Internet
 jain ne uske baad apane vichaar ko kaagaj par utaarne ke liye neshnal institute of dizin ke varisht chitrakaar sapan javeri se sampark saadhaa or use murtarup le lene par dak vibhaag se 1800 stamp chhapane kaa anurodh kiya
 The total cost for preparing the form of this ticket came to 75 thousand rupees, including 13 thousand rupees taken by the postal department
 pradeep se yah puche jane par ki vah in dak tikaton kaa kya karenge, unhone muskaraate hue kaha ki yah apni khushi ke liye kiya
 He will present this to those who would be willing to include Narendra Modi in the postage stamp collection
 uttar pradesh ke bulandshahr main kathith gokshi ke baad hui hinsa ke maamle main ek or video viral hua he
 In this video, Sumit, a youth killed during the violence, is seen stoning the police along with other youths

 1
 Evidence cannot replace evidence as deep as doubt

 The presumption should not be made into a reality and the judgment should reflect transparency

 The verdict should not be based on the facts themselves

 Wrong to look at evidence from a narrow perspective

 Evidence, facts should not dominate your thinking
